Armor of the Fang
Cowl of the Fang
(2) Set:
Increases your attack and casting speed by 1%.
(3) Set:
Increases damage done by Nature spells and effects by up to 14.
(3) Set:
Increases healing done by spells and effects by up to 22.
(4) Set:
+10 Intellect.
(5) Set:
When your health drops below 35%, you rapidly heal 90 health over 5 sec. This effect can trigger only once every 3 min.
(6) Set:
Your Cat Form seems to react to the full embrace of the Viper.
